66018001	Lacen dok aneno lamalaika mukene ka lor piny kun a ki i polo , ma onoŋo tye ki twero madit ; deyone oryeny ocaro wi lobo ducu .
66018002	Ci odaŋŋe ma dwane winnye matek twatwal ni , “ Babilon madit doŋ opoto , opoto gire woko ! Doŋ odoko kabedo pa jogi , odoko bene ka kanne pa cen maraco ducu , ki pa winyo maraco ma i dano kwero .
66018003	Rok ducu gumato koŋo vino me timme macol me tarwaŋ ca , luker ducu me wi lobo gutimo kwede abor , ki lucat-wil ma i wi lobo ducu doŋ gumedde gudoko lulonyo pi bedone me caro ki tim twarwaŋe-ni ma okato kare . ”
66018004	Dok awinyo dwan mukene ma oa ki ipolo kun wacci , “ Wun jona , wua woko ki bote , wek pe wuribbe kwede i balle , wek bene pe wunywak kwede gemo mogo ma poto i kome !
66018005	Pien balle doŋ odurre malo lipim , oo wa i polo , Lubaŋa doŋ opo i kom tim maraco ducu ma yam en otimo .
66018006	Wutim dako-nu ki kit tim ma yam en otimowu kwede , ma en otimo , wurub gin ma en mato obed mapek twatwal i kikopone kikome ma ya en orubo iye ginamata botwu-ni .
66018007	Dok wumi bote arem ki kumo ma rom ki kit ma en obedo ka wakke kwede , ki timme me caro caro . Pien en waco ki i cwinye ni , ‘ An daker , abedo i wi kom , pe arom ki da-to , pe abibedo ki kumo wacel ’ ,
66018008	pi meno gemone ducu bipoto i kome i nino acel , two odeke , kumo ki kec . Gibiwaŋe woko bene ki mac , pien Rwot Lubaŋa ma ŋolo kop i kome tekke dit . ”
66018009	Doŋ luker me wi lobo ma yam gutimo abor kwede , ma gulubo timme me tarwaŋ , gibikok pire kun gidoŋo oduru ma noŋo ginene doŋ tye ka waŋ i mac kun yitone duny .
66018010	Gibicuŋ wa cen pi lworo kit can ma giune kwede , kun giwacci , “ Ai do , ai do ! Ineno can ba , in Babilon , gaŋ madit dok matek ! Kop ma giŋolo i komi doŋ opoto i komi lawaŋacel . ”
66018011	Lucat-wil me lobo bene gitye ka koko kun gikumo pire , pien ŋat mo pe ma dok biwilo jami ma opoŋ i melgi ,
66018012	jabu , ryal , litino kidi me wel , tiko matar me wel , boŋo camanini maberre , boŋŋi ma obedo lamar lamar , boŋŋi aridi ki makwar , ki kit bao mapatpat ducu ma ŋwecgi kur , jami ducu ma gitiyo ki lak lyec-gu , jami ducu ma gitiyogi ki bao ma welgi malo twatwal , mola , nyonyo , ki got me gedo ma giliyo aliya maber twatwal ,
66018013	cinamon ki gin mogo mukene ma ŋwecgi kur , odok eceta me awaŋa , murra , odok luban , koŋo vino , moo jeituni , moko mapwot ki ŋano , dyaŋi ki romi , aguragura , ki gadigadi lweny , opii , kadi wa kwo pa dano kikome .
66018014	“ Nyig yat ma yam cwinyi paro twatwal-li doŋ gikwanyo woko ki boti , cam mogo mamit ma pe nen atata ki jami ma gipwoyo ki waŋ , doŋ gurwenyo woko ki boti , pe dok ibinoŋogi matwal ! ”
66018015	Lucat-wil ma yam gicato jami magi ducu , ma doŋ gudoko lulonyo pi gaŋ meno , gibicuŋ wa cen ka mabor pi lworo ki can ma giune kwede , kun gikok matek ma kumo kwede ni ,
66018016	“ Ai do , ai do , gaŋ madit-ti oneno can ba , en gaŋ ma yam onoŋo giruko woko ki boŋo camanini maberre , ki boŋŋi ma lamar lamar ki makwar , kun gidero woko ki jabu , kidi me wel , ki tiko matar me wel bene .
66018017	Lonyo madit kit man-ni giketo woko teŋteŋ lawaŋacel . ” Ludito me mel , ki jo ma woto i nam , ludwo mel ki jo ducu ma gitiyo tic me cato wil i nam , gucuŋ wa cen ka mabor ,
66018018	ci gudaŋŋe matek ka gunene tye ka waŋ kun yito duny , kun giwacci , “ Gaŋ mene ma onoŋo yam rom ki gaŋ man madit-ti ? ”
66018019	Ciguonyo putu i wigi , i kare ma gitye ka koko kun gikumo ma gidaŋŋe ki koko matek pire ni , “ Ai do , ai do , ineno can ba , in gaŋ madit-ti , ka ma jo ducu ma yam gitye ki melgi i nam gudoko lulonyo pi lonyone madwoŋŋi ! Giketo woko teŋteŋ i cawa acel keken .
66018020	Wudaŋŋe ki wer me yomcwiny , wun lwak me polo , wun jo maleŋ , wun lukwena ki lutit lok pa Lubaŋa , pien Lubaŋa doŋ odwoko kop ma yam oŋolo i komwu-ni i kome ! ”
66018021	Lalaikmaa mo matek otugi kwanyo gweŋ mo madit ma rom ki kidi rego , ci obolo woko i nam , kun wacci , “ Babilon ma en gaŋ madit-ti gibitimo ki tim bwami gicanyo woko matek i ŋom , pe doŋ gibinoŋo matwal !
66018022	Dwan lugo-naŋa ki jo ma goyo wer ducu , dwan lukut nyamulere ki lukut tum pe dok biwinnye boti matwal . Dano mo ma tiyo tic me diro pe dok binoŋŋe boti matwal . Mor pa kidi rego pe dok biwinnye boti matwal .
66018023	Tara mo pe dok bilyel menyi , kadi ki dwan lanyom ki dwan nyako ger pe dok biwinnye boti matwal ; pien lucat-willi onoŋo yam gin jo ma pigi dito atika i lobo yam bene ibwolo rok ducu ki tim jokjok ma ibedo ka timone .
66018024	Remo pa lutit lok pa Lubaŋa ki pa jo maleŋa , remo pa jo ducu ma yam ginekogi i lobo , ginoŋo tye i Babilon . ”
66019001	Lacen i ŋe man awinyo woo madwoŋ macalo dwan lwak dano mapol ata ma gktye i polo ma giwacci , “ Aleluya ! Laro dano ki deyo ki teko tye bot Lubaŋawa ,
66019002	pien kop ma en ŋolo ducu tye ada dok atir . En doŋ oŋolo kop woko i kom dako ma malaya-ni , ma yam obalo lobo woko ki timme me abor-ri , dok bene oculo kwor me remo pa luticce i kome . ”
66019003	Gin dok gudaŋŋe tyen me aryone kun giwacci , “ Aleluya ! Yito me waŋo gaŋ-ŋi duny mucido cito malo lituu nakanaka . ”
66019004	Ci ludoŋo pyeraŋwen-ni kacel ki lee makwo aŋwen-ni guryebbe woko piny guworo Lubaŋa ma obedo i wi komkerri , kun giwacci , “ Amen . Aleluya ! ”
66019005	Dwan mo dok oa ki i wi komker ma wacci , “ Wupak Lubaŋa , wun luticce ducu , wun jo ma wulwore , jo matino wa ki jo madito . ”
66019006	Ka dok awinyo dwan mo ma winnye calo lwak madit ma giwo , calo mor pa pii ma corre , dok calo mor kot ma mwoc matek . Guwacci , “ Aleluya ! Pien Rwot Lubaŋawa Won Twer Ducu , tye ka loc .
66019007	Wabedu ki yomcwiny , kun wadwore , dok bene wami deyo bote , pien kare me nyom pa Latin romo doŋ oo , nyako gerre bene doŋ oyubbe woko ;
66019008	gimiyo boŋo camanini maberre ma ryeny dok maleŋ en aye ni en oruki . ” Pien boŋo camanini maberre-nu obedo gin ducu ma tye atir ma jo maleŋ gitimo .
66019009	Ci lamalaika owacca ni , “ Co lok man ni , Jo ma gilwoŋogi i karama pa Latin romo tye ki gum . ” Dok owacca ni , “ Lok magi lok pa Lubaŋa . ”
66019010	Cutcut aryebbe woko piny ka tyene ka wore , ento en owacca ni , “ Pe myero itim kit meno ! An latic wadiwu , dok arom ki utmegini ma gumako lok me caden ma Yecu omiyo botgi-ni . Wor Lubaŋa . ” Pien lok me caden ma Yecu omiyo aye cwiny ma miyo lutit lok gitito lok pa Lubaŋa
66019011	Lacen aneno polo oyobbe , cut atugi neno aguragura matar ! Ŋat ma obedo i wiye gilwoŋo ni ŋat ma Genne dok me Ada , gin ma en timo ducu tye atir i ŋolo kop kadi wa i lweny bene .
66019012	Waŋe ryeny calo mac , dok onoŋo oruko lalukana mapol me loc i wiye ; onoŋo bene tye ki nyiŋ mo ma gigoro ma ŋat mo pe ŋeyo , kono en keken gire aye ŋeyo .
66019013	Oruko boŋo ma onoŋo giluto i remo , dok nyiŋ ma onoŋo gilwoŋe kwede en aye Lok pa Lubaŋa .
66019014	Lwak mony mapol me polo ma guruko boŋo camanini maberre , matar dok maleŋ , gulubo kore ma giriŋo ki aguragura matar .
66019015	Pala lucan mabit okatti ki i dogge , ma en bineko ki lurok woko ducu , ka doŋ bibedo ka loyogi ki odoo nyonyo ; en binyono bur me biyo koŋo vino me akemo pa Lubaŋa mager ma en Won Twer Ducu-ni .
66019016	Onoŋo gicoyo nyiŋ i kom jorre ki i eme ma kwanne ni , Kabaka ma loyo luker ducu ki Rwot pa rwodi .
66019017	Ka dok aneno lamalaika mo ocuŋ i ceŋ . En olwoŋo kwa winyo ducu mapatpat ma gituk i dye yamo ki dwan maloŋo ni , “ Wubin , wugurre kacel ka camo cam me otyeno ma Lubaŋa oyubo ,
66019018	ka camo riŋo kom luker , ki riŋo kom ludito wi mony , ki riŋo kom jo ma yam gin oteka , riŋo aguragura ki riŋo kom jo ma ŋweco kwedgi , ki riŋo dano ducu , jo ma gilone kengi kacel ki opii , jo matino ki madito ducu . ”
66019019	Lacen aneno lee ca ki luker me lobo guywayo monygi me lweny i kom ŋat ma obedo i wi aguragura kacel ki monnye .
66019020	Ento gimako lee ca woko , kacel ki lanebi ma lagoba , ma yam obedo ka tiyo tic mogo me aura i nyime , ma obwolo dano ma onoŋo doŋ giketo poyo pa lee ca i komgi , ki ma yam onoŋo giworo calle-ni . Gin aryo-nu ducu , lee ki lanebi ma lagoba , gibologi woko makwo i nam me mac , ma tye ka lyel ki gweŋ calfa ma mac oliyo .
66019021	Jo mudoŋŋe ducu ginekogi woko ki pala lucwan pa ŋat ma obedo i wi aguragura matar-ri , ki pala lucan ma okatti ki i doge ; winyo ducu guyeŋ woko ki riŋo kom dano ma gucamo .
66020001	Ka dok aneno lamalaika mo oa ki i polo kun lor bino piny ; onoŋo omako layab me bur ma tere pe gik , ki nyor mapek adada .
66020002	Ci omako min kulu madit ca , ma obedo twol macon-ni , ma en aye Ladot dok Catan bene , ka otweye woko pi mwaka alip acel ,
66020003	ci obole woko i bur ma tere pe gik , oloro dog bur woko , omwono woko bene kun oketo lanen i wiye wek pe dok omedde ki bwolo rok ducu , nio waŋ ma mwaka alip acel doŋ okato . I ŋe meno myero gigonye woko pi kare mo manoknok .
66020004	Lacen dok aneno kamker mapol , jo ma gubedo i wigi obedo jo ma onoŋo gimiyo botgi twero me ŋolo kop . Aneno bene tipo pa jo ma yam giŋolo ŋutgi woko pi miyo cadengi i kom Yecu ki pi lok pa Lubaŋa , gin jo ma yam pe guworo lee ca , nyo calle , dok bene ma yam pe guketo poyone i tur nyimgi nyo i ciŋgi . Gin doki gubedo kwo , gubedo ka loc kacel ki Kricito pi mwaka alip acel .
66020005	Jo muto mukene-gu ducu pe dok gubedo kwo , nio waŋ ma mwaka alip acel doŋ okato . Man aye cer mukwoŋo .
66020006	Tye ki gum ŋat ma bibedo i cer man mukwoŋo-ni , dok bene en dano maleŋ pa Lubaŋa kikome . Jo macalo meno , to me aryo pe tye ki twero mo i komgi , ento gin doŋ gibibedo ajwagi pa Lubaŋa ki pa Yecu , dok bene gibibedo ka loc kacel kwede pi mwaka alip acel .
66020007	Ka inen mwak alip acel doŋ otum , ci gibigonyo Catan woko ki i mabucce .
66020008	Ci en bikatti woko cito ka bwolo rok ducu ma tye i but piny , ma en aye Gog ki Magog , bicokogi bene pi lweny , jo ma welgi pe kwanne ma girom ki kweyo me dog nam .
66020009	Gumol gucito guket woko i wi lobo ka malac ci gurumo gony pa jo pa Lubaŋa ki gaŋ ma en maro-ni , ento mac oa ki i polo ci owaŋogi woko liweŋ .
66020010	Catan ma yam obwologi-ni bene gibolo woko i nam me mac ki gweŋ calfa ma mac oliyo , ka ma lee ki lanebi ma lagoba bene gitye iye ca ; gibibedo ki arem nakanaka dyeceŋ ki dyewor .
66020011	Dok aneno komker mo madit matar , ki ŋat ma obedo i wiye . Lobo ki polo gua ki i nyime guriŋo woko , ento pe dok ginoŋo kabedo mo pigi .
66020012	Ci aneno jo muto , jo madito ki jo matino , kun gucuŋ i nyim komker , onoŋo bene tye kenyo buk mogo ma giyabo igi woko . Giyabo bene buk mo mukene ma en aye buk me kwo . Giŋolo kop i kom jo muto kun gilubo gin ma yam gin gutiyo , kit macalo onoŋo gicoyo i buk magi .
66020013	Nam bene odwoko jo ma yam guto i iye-ni woko cen , To ki Lyel bene gumiyo jo muto ma yam tye botgi ; ci giŋolo kop pa dano acel acel kun gilubo gin ma yam gin gutiyo .
66020014	Gibolo To ki Lyel woko i nam mac . Nam me mac aye meno to me aryo .
66020015	Gam mo ma yam pe ginoŋo nyiŋe gicoyo i buk me kwo , gibolo woko i nam me mac .
66021001	Lacen dok aneno polo manyen ki lobo manyen , pien polo mukwoŋo ki lobo mukwoŋo onoŋo doŋ gurwenyo woko , kadi wa nam bene onoŋo doŋ pe .
66021002	Ci aneno gaŋ maleŋ , Jerucalem manyen , kun oa ki i polo bot Lubaŋa bino piny , ma giyubo woko macalo nyako ger ma gideyo pi cware .
66021003	Ci awinyo dwan mo maloŋo ma oa ki i komker kun wacci , “ Nen , kabedo pa Lubaŋa doŋ tye bot dano . En bibedo kacel kwedgi , ci gin gibibedo jone . Lubaŋa kikome aye bibedo kwedgi , kun bene bedo Lubaŋagi .
66021004	En bijwayo pig waŋgi woko ducu . To bene doŋ bibedo pe , kadi kumo nyo koko , nyo arem , pien gin macon doŋ ducu gurwenyo woko matwal . ”
66021005	Ci ŋat ma obedo i wi komker owacci , “ Nen , aketo jami ducu doko nyen . ” Ka dok bene owacci , “ Co lok man , pien lok magi lok ma genne dok me ada . ”
66021006	Ci owacca ni , “ Doŋ otimme ! An Alupa ki Omega , an acakki ki agikki . Ŋat ma orwo neko , abimiyo mato pii me waŋ it me kwo laboŋo wel mo .
66021007	Meno aye mot ma ŋat ma oloyo binoŋo , ki an abibedo Lubaŋane , en bene bibedo latinna .
66021008	Ento jo ma lwor , ma pe gin lugen , lutim tim mogo me kwer , lunek dano , lutim abor , lutim tim jokjok , luwor cal jogi , ki jo ducu ma gin lugoba , gibinoŋo mot ma gipoko botgi i nam ma tye ka lyel mac ki gweŋ calfa ; meno aye to me aryo . ”
66021009	Ci malaika acel ki i kin lumalaika abiro ma onoŋo gitye ki atabo abiro ma gemo abiro me agikki tye i igi ca , obino oloko bota kun wacci , “ Bin , anyutti Nyako ger , dako pa Latin romo . ”
66021010	Cutcut otiŋa , otera woko wa i wi got mo madit mabor twatwal , kun onoŋo Cwiny Maleŋ doŋ oyuto tamma woko , ka onyutta Jerucalem , gaŋ maleŋ , ma oa ki i polo bot Lubaŋa bino piny ,
66021011	ma onoŋo tye ki deyo pa Lubaŋa . Onoŋo ryeny calo kidi me wel madit makato ducu , ma pe nen atata , calo jacipa , dok leŋ calo gweŋ ma mil amila .
66021012	Celle onoŋo dit ocudo malo likuŋ , doge onoŋo tye apar wiye aryo . Lumalaika apar wiye aryo onoŋo gitye i dogcel ducu , dok bene i dogcel onoŋo gicoyo iye nyiŋ kaka apar wiye aryo pa jo Icrael .
66021013	Dogcel adek onoŋo tye yo tuŋ wokceŋ , yo tuŋ acam dogcel adek , yo tuŋ acuc dogcel adek , ki yo tuŋ potoceŋ bene dogcel adek .
66021014	Cel me gaŋ bene onoŋo tye ki te gutine apar wiye aryo , ci i komgi onoŋo tye iye nyiŋ lukwena apar wiye aryo pa Latin romo .
66021015	Ŋat ma oloko kweda-ni onoŋo tye ki odoo lagada jabu me pimo gaŋ ki dogcel ki cel kikome .
66021016	Gaŋ meno onoŋo yam twoke tye aŋwen ma giromrom , borre rom ki lacce , ci opimo cel ki odoone , oromo mairo alip acel ki miya abic ; borre ki lacce ki borre ma odok malo ducu gubedo rom .
66021017	En bene dok opimo cel , ci oromo futi miya aryo ki apar wiye abicel ka gipimo ki bad dano , kit macalo lamalaika opimo kwede .
66021018	Cel onoŋo gigero ki jacipa , ki gaŋ mere gigero ki jabu keken , ma noŋo nen maleŋ calo kiyo .
66021019	Te guti ducu me gaŋ onoŋo gideyo woko ki litino kidi me wel mapatpat . Mukwoŋo obedo kidi ma gilwoŋo ni jacipa , me aryo capir , me adek agat , me aŋwen emeradi ,
66021020	me abic onik , me abicel karnelian , me abiro kuricolit , me aboro berul , me aboŋwen topaj , me apar kuricoparac , me apar wiye acel jacint , me apar wiye aryo ameticito .
66021021	Gin me loro dogcel apar wiye aryo-ni onoŋo obedo tiko matar me wel apar wiye aryo , gin me loro dogcel acel acel gitiyo ki kit tiko-nu acel keken ; yo ducu ma i gaŋ gipeto ki jabu keken , ma nen leŋ calo kiyo .
66021022	Pe aneno ot mo me woro Lubaŋa i gaŋ meno , pien ot me woro Lubaŋa ki kunnu en aye Rwot Lubaŋa Won Twer Ducu kikome , ki Latin romo .
66021023	Ceŋ nyo dwe pe bimitte i gaŋ meno me ryeny iye , pien deyo pa Lubaŋa aye leŋo ma tye kunnu , ki tarane en aye Latin romo .
66021024	Leŋo ma tye iye bimiyo rok ducu giwoto maber ; ki luker ducu ma i wi lobo gibikelo deyogi iye .
66021025	Pe gibiloro dogcelle i dyeceŋ , ki dyewor bene bibedo pe kunnu .
66021026	Gibitero iye deyo ki lonyo pa rok ducu .
66021027	Ento gin mo ma kome keni pe bidonyo iye , kadi ki ŋat mo ma timo gin me kwer , nyo gin me goba , ento kono jo ma nyiŋgi doŋ gicoyo woko i buk me kwo-ni keken .
66022001	Lamalaika dok onyutta kulu me pii me kwo , ma mil amila lamakmak calo gweŋ ma mil , ma onoŋo mol kun a ki i komker pa Lubaŋa ki pa Latin romo ,
66022002	onoŋo mol lubo dye yo me gaŋ meno . Dok bene i dog kulu ryoryo onoŋo yat me kwo tye iye , ma tye ki nyige mapatpat ma romo apar wiye aryo , onoŋo bene nyak dwe ki dwe . Pot yat meno onoŋo obedo yat me caŋo two pa jo me rok ducu .
66022003	Gin ma giceno pe dok binen kunnu , ento komker pa Lubaŋa ki pa Latin romo aye bibedo iye , ki luticce gibiwore .
66022004	Gibineno waŋe , ki nyiŋe bene bibedo i tur nyimgi .
66022005	Dyewor doŋ pe bibedo tye matwal ; pe dok gibimito mac ma caro piny , nyo ceŋ , pien Rwot Lubaŋa bibedo ceŋgi , ci gin gibibedo ka loc nakanaka .
66022006	Ka dok owacca ni , “ Lok magi lok ma genne , dok me ada . Rwot ma en Lubaŋa ma loyo cwiny lutit lokke doŋ ocwalo lamalaikane me nyuto bot luticce gin ma bitimme i kare macokcok-ki .
66022007	Nen , doŋ acok bino . ” Tye ki gum dano ma lubo lok ma gitito i buk man .
66022008	An aye Jon , ŋat ma yam owinyo lok man dok oneno gin magi ducu . I kare ma awinyo lok man dok ma anenogi , cutcut aryebbe woko piny ka tyen lamalaika ma onyutta gin magi ka amiye woro ;
66022009	ento en owacca ni , “ Pe myero itim kit meno ! An latic wadiwu , arom ki utmegini ma gin lutit lok pa Lubaŋa , ki jo ma gilubo lok ma gicoyo i buk man . Wor Lubaŋa . ”
66022010	Ka dok owacca ni , “ Pe imwon lok magi ma gitito i buk-ki woko , pien kare doŋ cok .
66022011	Wek lutim maraco koŋ gumedde ki timo gin marac jo ma cilo me bal obwoyogi gumedde ki bedo ki bal , ki jo ma kitgi atir myero gumedde ki timo gin ma tye atir , ki jo maleŋ bene myero pud gumedde ki bedo leŋ . ”
66022012	“ Nen , doŋ acok bino , kun akelo motta me pwoc , me culo dano acel acel muporo tic ma en otiyo .
66022013	An Alupa ki Omega , mukwoŋo ki me agikki , acakki ki agikki . ”
66022014	Jo ma lwoko ginarukagi wek gibed ki twero me camo nyig yat me kwo , ki me donyo i gaŋ ma noŋo giwok ki i dogcel , jo-nu aye tye ki gum .
66022015	I ŋe gaŋ woko tye iye jo ma timo tim calo gin gwogi , lutim tim jokjok , lutim abor , lunek dano , ki luwor cal jogi , ki jo ducu ma maro loko goba , kun gitiyo bene gin me gobagoba .
66022016	“ An Yecu doŋ acwalo lamalaikana me tito lok me caden botwu pi lwak jo muye an ducu ma gitye i kabedo ducu . An a lwit yat dok bene lakwar Daudi , an latwok ma ryeny twatwal-li . ”
66022017	Cwiny Maleŋ kacel ki nyako ger gitye ka wacci , “ Bin ! ” Ŋat ma owinyo lok man bene myero ogam ni , “ Bin ! ” Ŋat ma orwo neko myero obin , wek ŋat ma mito bene omat pii me kwo laboŋo wel .
66022018	Doŋ aciko jo ducu ma guwinyo lok ma gitito i buk man , ni , ka ce dano mo dok omedo lok mo iye , Lubaŋa bene bimedo gemo ma gitito pire i buk kany-nyi i kome .
66022019	Dok bene ka ce ŋat mo okwanyo lok mo woko ki i kom lok ma gitito i buk kany , Lubaŋa bene bikwanyo twerone me camo yat me kwo ki donyo i gaŋ maleŋ woko , ma gicoyo pigi i buk kany-nyi .
66022020	Ŋat ma miyo caden i kom lok magi bene owacci , “ Adada , binona doŋ cok . ” Amen . Rwot Yecu , bin !
66022021	Kica pa Rwot Yecu obed ki jo pa Lubaŋa ducu . Amen .
